<td style="padding:0.2em 0 0.4em"><a href="/wiki/File:Map_of_Darfur_2011.png" class="image"><img alt="Map of Darfur 2011.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Map_of_Darfur_2011.png/150px-Map_of_Darfur_2011.png" width="150" height="132" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Map_of_Darfur_2011.png/225px-Map_of_Darfur_2011.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Map_of_Darfur_2011.png/300px-Map_of_Darfur_2011.png 2x" data-file-width="2548" data-file-height="2250" /></a></td>

<th style="padding:0.1em;background:lightsteelblue;">Other articles</th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="padding:0 0.1em 0.4em">

<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;font-size:115%">
<div class="plainlinks hlist navbar mini">
<ul>
<li class="nv-view"><a href="/wiki/Template:War_in_Darfur" title="Template:War in Darfur"><abbr title="View this template">v</abbr></a></li>
<li class="nv-talk"><a href="/wiki/Template_talk:War_in_Darfur" title="Template talk:War in Darfur"><abbr title="Discuss this template">t</abbr></a></li>
<li class="nv-edit"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:War_in_Darfur&amp;action=edit"><abbr title="Edit this template">e</abbr></a></li>
</ul>
</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>The <b>War in Darfur</b> is a major armed conflict in the <a href="/wiki/Darfur" title="Darfur">Darfur</a> region of <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a>, that began in February 2003 when the <a href="/wiki/Sudan_Liberation_Movement/Army" title="Sudan Liberation Movement/Army">Sudan Liberation Movement</a> (SLM) and the <a href="/wiki/Justice_and_Equality_Movement" title="Justice and Equality Movement">Justice and Equality Movement</a> (JEM) rebel groups began fighting the <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Sudan" class="mw-redirect" title="Government of Sudan">government of Sudan</a>, which they accused of oppressing Darfur's non-<a href="/wiki/Arab" class="mw-redirect" title="Arab">Arab</a> population.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup> The government responded to attacks by carrying out a campaign of <a href="/wiki/Ethnic_cleansing" title="Ethnic cleansing">ethnic cleansing</a> against Darfur's non-Arabs. This resulted in the deaths of hundreds of thousands of civilians and the indictment of Sudan's president <a href="/wiki/Omar_al-Bashir" title="Omar al-Bashir">Omar al-Bashir</a> for <a href="/wiki/Genocide" title="Genocide">genocide</a>, <a href="/wiki/War_crime" title="War crime">war crimes</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Crimes_against_humanity" title="Crimes against humanity">crimes against humanity</a> by the <a href="/wiki/International_Criminal_Court" title="International Criminal Court">International Criminal Court</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup></p>
<p>One side of the conflict is composed mainly of Sudanese military and police and the <a href="/wiki/Janjaweed" title="Janjaweed">Janjaweed</a>, a Sudanese <a href="/wiki/Militia" title="Militia">militia</a> group recruited mostly among <a href="/wiki/Arabization" title="Arabization">Arabized</a> indigenous Africans and a small number of <a href="/wiki/Bedouin" title="Bedouin">Bedouin</a> of the northern <a href="/wiki/Rizeigat" class="mw-redirect" title="Rizeigat">Rizeigat</a>; the majority of other Arab groups in Darfur remained uninvolved.<sup id="cite_ref-guardian2004_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-guardian2004-22">[22]</a></sup> The other side is made up of rebel groups, notably the SLM/A and the JEM, recruited primarily from the non-Arab Muslim <a href="/wiki/Fur_people" title="Fur people">Fur</a>, <a href="/wiki/Zaghawa_people" title="Zaghawa people">Zaghawa</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Masalit_people" title="Masalit people">Masalit</a> ethnic groups. The <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> also have a joint <a href="/wiki/List_of_United_Nations_peacekeeping_missions" title="List of United Nations peacekeeping missions">peacekeeping mission</a> in the region, named <a href="/wiki/UNAMID" class="mw-redirect" title="UNAMID">UNAMID</a>. Although the Sudanese government publicly denies that it supported the Janjaweed, evidence supports claims that it provided financial assistance and weapons and coordinated joint attacks, many against civilians.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-UCDP_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UCDP-24">[24]</a></sup> Estimates of <a href="#Mortality_figures">the number of human casualties</a> range up to several hundred thousand dead, from either combat or starvation and disease. Mass displacements and coercive migrations forced millions into refugee camps or across the border, creating a <a href="/wiki/Humanitarian_crisis" title="Humanitarian crisis">humanitarian crisis</a>. Former US <a href="/wiki/Secretary_of_State" class="mw-redirect" title="Secretary of State">Secretary of State</a> <a href="/wiki/Colin_Powell" title="Colin Powell">Colin Powell</a> described the situation as a genocide or acts of genocide.<sup id="cite_ref-Jones2006_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jones2006-25">[25]</a></sup></p>
<p>The Sudanese government and the JEM signed a ceasefire agreement in February 2010, with a tentative agreement to pursue peace. The JEM has the most to gain from the talks and could see semi-autonomy much like <a href="/wiki/South_Sudan" title="South Sudan">South Sudan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup> However, talks were disrupted by accusations that the Sudanese army launched raids and air strikes against a village, violating the Tolu agreement. The JEM, the largest rebel group in Darfur, vowed to boycott negotiations.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup></p>
<table style="float: right; clear:right; margin: 0 0 0.5em 1em; padding: 0.5em; background: #fffff4; border: 1px solid #ddb; width: 200px; font-size:85%;">
